# Go API client for amplify

APIs to manage AMPLIFY Central configuration resources.

## Overview
This API client was generated by the [OpenAPI Generator](https://openapi-generator.tech) project.  By using the [OpenAPI-spec](https://www.openapis.org/) from a remote server, you can easily generate an API client.

- API version: 0.347.0
- Package version: 1.0.0
- Generator version: 7.7.0
- Build package: org.openapitools.codegen.languages.GoClientCodegen

## Installation

Install the following dependencies:

```sh
go get github.com/stretchr/testify/assert
go get golang.org/x/oauth2
go get golang.org/x/net/context
```

Put the package under your project folder and add the following in import:

```go
import amplify "github.com/aaron-axway/amplify-go-client"
```

To use a proxy, set the environment variable `HTTP_PROXY`:

```go
os.Setenv("HTTP_PROXY", "http://proxy_name:proxy_port")
```

## Configuration of Server URL

Default configuration comes with `Servers` field that contains server objects as defined in the OpenAPI specification.

### Select Server Configuration

For using other server than the one defined on index 0 set context value `amplify.ContextServerIndex` of type `int`.

```go
ctx := context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextServerIndex, 1)
```

### Templated Server URL

Templated server URL is formatted using default variables from configuration or from context value `amplify.ContextServerVariables` of type `map[string]string`.

```go
ctx := context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextServerVariables, map[string]string{
	"basePath": "v2",
})
```

Note, enum values are always validated and all unused variables are silently ignored.

### URLs Configuration per Operation

Each operation can use different server URL defined using `OperationServers` map in the `Configuration`.
An operation is uniquely identified by `"{classname}Service.{nickname}"` string.
Similar rules for overriding default operation server index and variables applies by using `amplify.ContextOperationServerIndices` and `amplify.ContextOperationServerVariables` context maps.

```go
ctx := context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextOperationServerIndices, map[string]int{
	"{classname}Service.{nickname}": 2,
})
ctx = context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextOperationServerVariables, map[string]map[string]string{
	"{classname}Service.{nickname}": {
		"port": "8443",
	},
})
```

*ManagementAPI* | [**UpdateManagementV1alpha1WatchTopicAccessControlListLanguages**](docs/ManagementAPI.md#updatemanagementv1alpha1watchtopicaccesscontrollistlanguages) | **Put** /management/v1alpha1/watchtopics/{watchtopicName}/accesscontrollists/{name}/languages | Update Languages data for AccessControlList for version v1alpha1 from group management in scope WatchTopic
*ManagementAPI* | [**UpdateManagementV1alpha1WatchTopicAccessControlListLanguagesCode**](docs/ManagementAPI.md#updatemanagementv1alpha1watchtopicaccesscontrollistlanguagescode) | **Put** /management/v1alpha1/watchtopics/{watchtopicName}/accesscontrollists/{name}/languages-{code} | Update Languages data for AccessControlList for version v1alpha1 from group management in scope WatchTopic
*ManagementAPI* | [**UpdateManagementV1alpha1WatchTopicExtension**](docs/ManagementAPI.md#updatemanagementv1alpha1watchtopicextension) | **Put** /management/v1alpha1/watchtopics/{name}/{extension} | Update Extension resource data of WatchTopic for version v1alpha1 from group management
*ManagementAPI* | [**UpdateManagementV1alpha1WatchTopicLanguages**](docs/ManagementAPI.md#updatemanagementv1alpha1watchtopiclanguages) | **Put** /management/v1alpha1/watchtopics/{name}/languages | Update Languages data for WatchTopic for version v1alpha1 from group management
*ManagementAPI* | [**UpdateManagementV1alpha1WatchTopicLanguagesCode**](docs/ManagementAPI.md#updatemanagementv1alpha1watchtopiclanguagescode) | **Put** /management/v1alpha1/watchtopics/{name}/languages-{code} | Update Languages data for WatchTopic for version v1alpha1 from group management

## Documentation For Authorization


Authentication schemes defined for the API:
### BearerToken

- **Type**: HTTP Bearer token authentication

Example

```go
auth := context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextAccessToken, "BEARER_TOKEN_STRING")
r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```

### OAuth2


- **Type**: OAuth
- **Flow**: implicit
- **Authorization URL**: https://login.axway.com/auth/realms/Broker/protocol/openid-connect/auth
- **Scopes**: N/A

Example

```go
auth := context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextAccessToken, "ACCESSTOKENSTRING")
r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```

Or via OAuth2 module to automatically refresh tokens and perform user authentication.

```go
import "golang.org/x/oauth2"

/* Perform OAuth2 round trip request and obtain a token */

tokenSource := oauth2cfg.TokenSource(createContext(httpClient), &token)
auth := context.WithValue(oauth2.NoContext, amplify.ContextOAuth2, tokenSource)
r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```

### OAuth2


- **Type**: OAuth
- **Flow**: application
- **Authorization URL**: 
- **Scopes**: N/A

Example

```go
auth := context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextAccessToken, "ACCESSTOKENSTRING")
r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```

Or via OAuth2 module to automatically refresh tokens and perform user authentication.

```go
import "golang.org/x/oauth2"

/* Perform OAuth2 round trip request and obtain a token */

tokenSource := oauth2cfg.TokenSource(createContext(httpClient), &token)
auth := context.WithValue(oauth2.NoContext, amplify.ContextOAuth2, tokenSource)
r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```

### OAuth2


- **Type**: OAuth
- **Flow**: accessCode
- **Authorization URL**: https://login.axway.com/auth/realms/Broker/protocol/openid-connect/auth
- **Scopes**: N/A

Example

```go
auth := context.WithValue(context.Background(), amplify.ContextAccessToken, "ACCESSTOKENSTRING")
r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```

Or via OAuth2 module to automatically refresh tokens and perform user authentication.

```go
import "golang.org/x/oauth2"

/* Perform OAuth2 round trip request and obtain a token */

tokenSource := oauth2cfg.TokenSource(createContext(httpClient), &token)
auth := context.WithValue(oauth2.NoContext, amplify.ContextOAuth2, tokenSource)
r, err := client.Service.Operation(auth, args)
```


## Documentation for Utility Methods

Due to the fact that model structure members are all pointers, this package contains
a number of utility functions to easily obtain pointers to values of basic types.
Each of these functions takes a value of the given basic type and returns a pointer to it:

* `PtrBool`
* `PtrInt`
* `PtrInt32`
* `PtrInt64`
* `PtrFloat`
* `PtrFloat32`
* `PtrFloat64`
* `PtrString`
* `PtrTime`

support@axway.com
